            <change when="2020-11-04" who="Dominik Wujastyk">Began this file.</change>
            <change when="2023-11-04" who="Dominik Wujastyk"> added 1.41, based on MS N</change>
            <change when="2023-06-26" who="Dominik Wujastyk">Separated the file into two parts, 1-31
                and 32-end, because of processing limits at Saktumiva</change>

            <change when="2023-10-25" who="Dominik Wujastyk">Added all remaining adhyāyas from H and
                stripped out transcription codes to make draft provisional edition files.</change>
            <change when="2024-03-27" who="Dominik Wujastyk">Completed a major overhaul
                ("meta-edit") of the all Sūtrasthāna files. I checked all passages and made sure
                that xml:id tags matched correctly across all files, unifying and separating
                text-portions as needed. I separated words ad hoc. I corrected readings and checked
                against the MSS in many cases, but again ad hoc. There is much remaining to be done,
                but the Sūtrasthāna is now in a coherent format at the macro scale.</change>

        <body>

            <div n="1" type="sthāna">


                <head xml:lang="en">[Sūtrasthāna 32-end]</head>

                <div n="32" type="adhyāya">

                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 32, draft based on MS H]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.32.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athātaḥ svabhāvavipratipattiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.3-4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.32.3-4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svabhāvaprasiddhānāṃ śarīraikadeśānām anyathātvaṃ maraṇāya | tad yathā
                        śuklānāṃ kṛṣṇatvaṃ kṛṣṇānāṃ śuklatvaṃ | sthirāṇām mṛdutvaṃ | calānām
                        acalatvam acalānāñ calatvaṃ | pṛthūnāṃ saṃkṣiptatvaṃ saṃkṣiptānāṃ pṛthutvaṃ
                        | dīrghāṇāṃ hrasvatvaṃ ca hrasvānāṃ dīrghatā | apatanadharmmiṇāṃ patanam
                        akasmāc chaityoṣṇasneharaukṣyaprastambhavaivarṇṇyāni apasarppaṇam aṅgānāṃ
                        svebhyaḥ sthānebhyaḥ śarīraikadeśānām
                        avasraṃsotkṣiptabhrāntapatitavimuktanirggamātigamagurulaghutvāni
                        pravālavarṇṇavyaṅgaprādurbbhāvo vākasmāt sirāṇāṃ ca darśana lalāṭe nāsāvaṃśe
                        vā piṭakotpattir udakotpattir nnetrarogam vināsrupravṛttir lalāṭe vā
                        prabhātakāle svedapravṛttiḥ | gomayacūrṇṇaprakāśasya rajaso darśanam
                        uttamāṅge līyanam vā kapotakaṅkagṛddhraprabhṛtīnāṃ mūtrapurīṣapravṛddhir
                        abhuñjanānāṃ stanamūlahṛdayorassu ca śūlotpattayaḥ | madhye śūnatvam anteṣu
                        parimlāyitvaṃ | viparyayo vā naṣṭahīnavikalavihṛtasvaraṃ vā
                        vivarṇṇapuṣpaprādurbbhāvo vā dantanakhaśarīreṣu puṣpadarśanaṃ yasya cāpsu
                        kaphaśakṛdretāṃsi nimajjanti yasya ca dṛṣṭimaṇḍale bhinnavikṛtāni rūpāṇy
                        ālocyante snehābhyaktakeśāṅga iva yo bhāti yaś ca durbbalo
                        bhaktadveṣātisārābhyām pīḍyate | kāsamānaś ca tṛṣṇātibhūtaḥ kṣīṇaś
                        charddibhaktadeśayuktaḥ saphenarudhirodvāmī hatasvaraḥ śūlābhihataś ca
                        manuṣyaśūnakaracaraṇo nnadveṣī srastapiṇḍakāṃsapāṇipādaḥ | yaś ca pūrvāhṇe
                        bhuktam aparāhṇe ścharddayaty avidagdhaṃ sāryate vā jvarakāsābhibhūtaḥ sa
                        śvāsān mriyate | vastavad vilapamāno bhūmau patati srastamuṣkaḥ stabdhaśepo
                        bhagnagrīvaḥ praṇaṣṭamehaś ca manuṣyaḥ prāgviśuṣyamāṇahṛdaya ārddraśarīraḥ |
                        yaś ca loṣṭaṃ loṣṭenābhihanti | kāṣṭham vā kāṣṭhena tṛṇāni vā cchinnanti |
                        adharoṣṭham vā daśati uttaroṣṭham vā leḍhi | āluñcati karṇṇau keśām̐ś ca |
                        devadvijagurusuhṛdvaidyān vā vidveṣṭi yasya ca vakrānuvakragā grahā
                        garhitasthānagatāḥ | janmaṛkṣam vāsyolkāśanibhyām abhihanyate | rātrau vā
                        gṛhadvāraśayanāsanayānavāhanamaṇiratnopakaraṇagarhitalakṣaṇanimittaprādurbbhāvo
                        veti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.32.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanti cātra ||
                        <caesura/>
                         cikitsyamānaḥ samyak tu vikāro yo 'bhivarddhate |
                        <caesura/>
                         prakṣīṇabala<pc> </pc>māṃsasya lakṣaṇan tadgatāyuṣaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.32.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nivarttate mahāvyādhiḥ sahasā yasya dehinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         na cāhāraphalaṃ yasya dṛśyate sa vinaśyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.32.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         etāni riṣṭarūpāṇi samyag budhyeta yo bhiṣak |
                        <caesura/>
                         sādhyāsādhyaparīkṣañ ca sa rājñaḥ sammato bhaved iti || 31 || ❈ || </l>

                </div>

                <div n="33" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 33, draft based on MS H]</head>




                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.1">
                        <label>1.33.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto vāraṇīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.33.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         upadravais tu ye juṣṭā-vyādhayo yānty avāryatāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rasāyanair vvinā vatsa tāṃ śṛṇv ekamanā mama || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.33.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vātavyādhiḥ pramehaś ca kuṣṭhānyatha bhagandaraṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         arśośmarī mūḍhagarbho bhavaty udaram aṣṭamam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.33.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         aṣṭāv ete mahāntaḥ syūr vvyādhayo dustarāḥ sadā | prāṇamāṃsakṣayaḥ śophas
                        tṛṣṇā ccharddir jvaras tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.33.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atīsāraś ca mūrcchā ca hikkāśvāsas tathaiva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         etair upadravair jjuṣṭān sarvvān etān vivarjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.33.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śūnaṃ suptatvacam bhagnaṅ kampādhmānanipīḍitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rujārttam antañ ca naram vātavyādhir vvināśayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.33.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathoktopadravāviṣṭam atiprasrutam eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         piṭakāpīḍitaṃ gāḍhaṃ prameho hanti mānavaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.33.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prabhinnaṃ prasrutāṅgañ ca raktanetraṃ hatasvaraṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pañcakarmmaguṇātītaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ hanti hi kuṣṭhinaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.33.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vātamūtrapurīṣāṇi krimayaḥ śukram eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhagandarāt prasravanti sa naśyati bhagandarī || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.33.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tṛṣṇarocakaśūlārttam atiprasrutaśoṇitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śophātīsārasaṃyuktaṃ durnāmā kṣapayen naraṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.33.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         praśūnanābhivṛṣaṇaṃ vaddhamūtrarujāturaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         aśmarī kṣapayaty āśu sikatāśarkkarānvitaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.33.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pārśvabhaṅgānnavidveṣaḥ śophātīsārapīḍitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vivarjayed udariṇam virikto yo 'bhipūryate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.33.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yonīsamvaraṇaṃ saṅgaḥ kukṣo makkallasaṃjñitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         hanyuḥ striyaṃ mūḍhaga-rvbhe yathoktāś cāpy upadravāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.33.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         visaṃjñas tām yate yas tu śete nipati-to yathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śītārddito 'ntaruṣṇaś ca jvareṇa mriyate naraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.33.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yo hṛṣṭaromā raktākṣo hṛdi saṃghātaśūlavān |
                        <caesura/>
                         vaktreṇa cocchvasiti taṃ jvaro hanti mānavaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.33.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hikkāśvāsa samāyuktaṃ mūḍham vibhrāntalocanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         santatocchvāsinaṃ kṣīṇaṃ naraṃ kṣapayate jvaraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.18"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.33.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śvāsaśūlapipāsārtaṃ-kṣīṇañ jvaranipīḍitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśeṣeṇa naraṃ vṛddham atīsāro vināśayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.33.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śuklākṣamannadveṣṭāram ūrddhaśvāsanipīḍitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛcchreṇa bahu mehantaṃ yakṣmā hantīha mānavaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.21">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.33.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śvāsaśūlapipāsānnavidveṣo granthimūḍhatā |
                        <caesura/>
                         jāyate durvvalatvaṃ ca gulmino maraṇāya vai|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.22">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.33.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ādhmānaṃ vaddhaniṣyandaṃ ccharddihikkātṛṣānvitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         rujāśvāsasamāyuktaṃ vidradhir nnāśayet naraṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.23">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.33.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pāṇḍudantanakho yastu pāṇḍunetraś ca mānavaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pāṇḍusaṃghātadarśī ca pāṇḍurogī vinaśyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.24">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.33.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         lohitañ charddayed yas tu bahuśo lohitekṣaṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         lohito 'ṅgāradarśī ca mriyate raktapaittikaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.25">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.33.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         avāco pi savāco 'pi kṣīṇamānsavalo naraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         jāgarūko kṣyāsandeham unmādena vinaśyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.26">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.33.26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         apasmarantam bahuśaḥ prakṣīṇañ calitaṃ bhruvaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         netrābhyāñ ca vikurvvāṇam apasmāro vināśayet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.trailer"> 33 ||</l>

                </div>

                <div n="34" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 34, draft based on MS H]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.1">
                        <label>1.34.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto yuktasenīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.1.1">
                        <label>1.34.1.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dhanvantarim mahāprājñaṃ sarvvaśāstraviśāradaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         caraṇāv upasaṃgṛhya suśrutaḥ paripṛcchati ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.34.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yuktasenasya nṛpateḥ parānabhijighāṃsataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhiṣajā rakṣaṇaṃ kāryaṃ yathā tad brūhi me mune ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.3.1">
                        <label>1.34.3.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā prābravīd bhiṣajām varaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.34.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vijigīṣuḥ sahāmātyair yātrāyuktaḥ prayatnataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rakṣitavyo viśeṣeṇa viṣādeva narādhipaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.34.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         panthānam udakañ chāyāṃ bhaktaṃ yavasamindhanaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         duṣayanty arayas tāni jānīyāc chodhanīya ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya liṅgaṃ cikitsāñ ca kalpasthāne pravakṣyate ||</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.34.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ekottaraṃ mṛtyuśatam atharvvāṇaḥ pracakṣate |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatraikaḥ kālasaṃyuktaḥ śeṣās tv āgantavaḥ smṛtāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.34.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣāgantunimittebhyo rasamantraviśāradau |
                        <caesura/>
                         rakṣatāṃ nṛpatin nityaṃ yatnād vaidyapurohitau ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.34.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         brahmāvedāṅgamaṣṭāṅgam āyurvvedam pracakṣate |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāt purohitamate vartteta bhiṣag ātmavān ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.34.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saṅkaraḥ sarvvavarṇṇānāṃ vināśo dharmmakarmmiṇāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         prajanām api kṛcchrāṇi bhavanti nṛpanāśataḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.34.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         puruṣāṇān nṛpānāñ ca kevalan tulyamūrttitā |
                        <caesura/>
                         ājñātyāgaḥ kṣamā dhairyam vikramaś cāpy amānuṣaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.34.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmād devam ivābhīkṣṇam vāṅmanaḥ karmabhiḥ śubhaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         cintayet nṛpatim vaidyaḥ śreyāṃsīcchan vicakṣaṇaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.34.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         skandhāvāre ca mahati rājaveśma samīpataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavet sannihito vaidyaḥ sarvvopakaraṇānvitaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.34.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrastham enan dhvajavad yaśaḥkhyātibhir ucchritaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         upasarppantyamohena viṣaśalyāmayārdditāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.34.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svatantrakuśalo 'nyeṣu śāstrārtheṣv abahiḥ kṛtaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vaidyo dhvajam ivābhāti nṛpatadvidyapūjitaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.34.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vaidyo vyādhyupasṛṣṭaś ca bhaiṣajam paricārakaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ete pādāś cikitsāyāḥ karmmasādhanahetavaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.34.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         guṇavadbhis tribhiḥ pādaiś caturthyo guṇavān bhiṣak |
                        <caesura/>
                         vyādhim alpena kālena mahāntam api sādhayet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.34.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vaidyahīnās trayaḥ pādā guṇavanto 'pyapārthakāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         udgātṛhotṛbrahmāṇo yathādhvaryam vinādhvare ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.34.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vaidyas tu guṇavāneko yāpayed āturaṃ sadā |
                        <caesura/>
                         plavam paricaran dhīraḥ karṇṇadhāram ivāmbhasi ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.34.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatvopagataśāstrārtho dṛṣṭakarmmā svayaṅkṛtī |
                        <caesura/>
                         laghuhastaḥ śuciḥ sūraḥ sajjopaskarabheṣajaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.34.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pratyutpannamatir ddhīmān vyavasāyī viśāradaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         satyadharmmaparo yaś ca sabhiṣak pāda ucyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.21">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.34.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āyuṣmān satvavān sādhyo dravyavān mitravān api |
                        <caesura/>
                         vaidyavākyakṛd āstiṣko vyādhitaḥ pāda ucyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.22">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.34.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         praśastadeśasaṃbhūtaṃ praśaste kāla uddhṛtaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yuktamātram manaskāntaṅ gandhavarṇṇarasānvitaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.23">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.34.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣaghnamaglāninikaram avikārya viparyayaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         samīkṣya dattaṅ kāle ca bheṣajam pāda ucyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.24">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.34.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snigdho 'jugupsur bbalavānyukto vyādhitarakṣaṇe |
                        <caesura/>
                         vaidyavākyakṛdaśrāntaḥ pādaḥ paricaraḥ smṛtaḥ ||</l>

                    <p ana="trailer">layka ||</p>
                </div>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.35.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāta āturopakramaṇīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.2"/>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.35.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āturam upakramamāṇena vaidyenāyurādāv eva tāvat parīsatyāyuṣi
                        vyādhyṛtvagnivayodehasatvavalasātmyaprakṛtibheṣajadeśān parīkṣeta | </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.35.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra
                        mahāpāṇipādapṛṣṭhastanāgrasukhadarśanaskandhalalāṭadīrghāṅguliparvvocchvāsaprekṣaṇavāhum
                        vistīrṇṇabhrūs tanāntaroraskaṃ hṛsvajaṅghāmeḍhragrīvaṅ
                        gambhīrasatvasvaranāsimanuccair vaddhas tanm upacitamahāromaṃ romasakarṇṇe
                        pārśva mastakaṃ snātānuliptaṃ mūrddham ānūpūrvyo paścāc ca
                        viśuṣyamāṇahṛdayam puruṣañ jānīyād dīrghāyuḥ khalv ayam iti | tam ekāntena
                        upakramet | tatra tail laikṣaṇair viparītair alpayum miśrair mmadhyam āyur
                        iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.35.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanti cātra ||
                        <caesura/>
                         gūḍhasandhisirāsnāyuḥ saṃhatāṅgaḥ sthirendriyaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         uttarottarasukṣetro yaḥ sa dīrghāyur ucyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.6">

                        <caesura/>
                         garbhāt prabhṛtyarogo yaḥ śanaiḥ samabhivarddhate |
                        <caesura/>
                         śarīrajñānavijñānaiḥ sa dīrghāyuḥ samāsataḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.35.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         madhyamasyāyuṣo jñāna mata ūrdhvan nibodha me |
                        <caesura/>
                         adhastād akṣayor yasya rekhāḥ suvyaktam āyatāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.8">

                        <caesura/>
                         dve vā tisro 'dhikā vāpi pādau karṇau ca māṃsalau |
                        <caesura/>
                         nāsāgram ūrdhvañ ca bhavet rekhāś ca pṛṣṭhataḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.9">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.10">

                        <caesura/>
                         avalīḍham uroyaś ca na ca syāt pṛṣṭham āyataṃ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.11">

                        <caesura/>
                         hasato jalpato vāpi dantamānsam pradṛśyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.12ab">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.35.12ab</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atha punar āyuṣo vijñānārtham aṅgapratyaṅgapramāṇasāra anupadekṣyāmaḥ ||
                        tatra aṅgātyantarādhiśakthivāhuśirāṃsi tad avayavāḥ pratyaṅgāni svair
                        aṅgulaiḥ pādāṅguṣṭhapradeśinyau dvaṅgulāyate | pradeśinyās tu
                        madhyamānāmikākaniṣṭhikā pūrvvataḥ | pañcañ bhāgahīnācaturaṅgulāyate |
                        pañcaṅgulavismṛte | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.18">

                        <caesura/>
                         vyādhiviśeṣās tu prāg abhihitāḥ sarvvaṃ evaite trividhā bhavanti | sādhyā
                        yāpyāḥ pratyākhyeyāś ceti | tatra sādhya yāpya pratyākhye yān vyādhīn
                        bhūyatri vidhā parīkṣeta | kimayam aupasargikaḥ prāk kevalo 'nyalakṣaṇa iti
                        | taraupasargiko nāma yaḥ pūrvvotpannaṃ vyādhiñ jaghanyakālajāto vyādhir
                        upasṛjati | sa tat mūle sa evopadravasaṃjñaḥ | prāk kevalo nāma | yaḥ
                        prāgevotpanno vyādhirar apūrvarūpopadravaś ca | anya lakṣaṇo nāma yo
                        bhaviṣyat khyāpakaḥ sa pūrvvarūpasaṃjñaḥ | tatra sopadravam
                        anyonyāvirodhenopacaret | valavantaram upadravam vā prāk kevalaṃ yathāsvam
                        pratikurvīta | anye lakṣaṇe tv ādivyādhau yathā yathāvat prayateta | </l>

                         prāg abhihito 'gnir annābhipācakaḥ sa pañcavidho bhavati || samo
                        doṣābhipanno vikriyām āpanna iti || viṣamo vātena | tīkṣṇa pittena | mandaḥ
                        śleṣmaṇā | samaḥ sarvvaiḥ samar iti || tatra yo yathā kālam annam upayuktaṃ
                        samya pacati sa samaḥ | yas tu kadācit samyak pacati kadācid asamyak pacaty
                        ādhmānaśūlātīsārapravāhaṇāni kṛtvā pacati sa viṣamaḥ | yas tu prabhūtam apy
                        annam upayuktam āśu pacati sa tīkṣṇaḥ | sarvābhivardhamāno 'tyagnir bhavati
                        || muhumr mmuhuḥ prabhūtataram annam upayuktam āśutaraṃ pacati pākānte ca
                        galatālvoṣṭhapraśoṣadāhasantāpān janayati asyaiva bhasmaka iti vyapadiśanti
                        || yas tv alpam apy annam upayuktam
                        udaraśirogauravakāsaśvāsacchardiprasekagātrasadanāni kṛtvā mahā kālena
                        pacati sa mandaḥ || bha || </l>

                        <caesura/>

                        kriyāviśeṣair upacaret || tīkṣṇam madhurasnigdhayuktair vvirecanaiś ca |
                        evam evāty agnim viśeṣeṇa māhiyaird dadhikṣīrasarppibhir iti || mande
                        kaṭutiktakaṣāyair vvamanaiś ca || bha || </l>

                        vālābhavanti | te trividhāḥ kṣīrapāḥ kṣīrānnādā annādā iti | ṣoḍaśasaptatyor
                        antare madhyasvayas tasyad vikalpo vṛddhir yauvanaṃ sampūrṇṇateti |
                        tatrāviṃśater vṛddhir ātriṃśato yauvanam ācatvāriṃśataḥ
                        sarvvadhātvindriyasampūrṇṇetiti || ata ūrdhvaṃ hā nir bhavati yāvadā
                        saptateḥ | saptatyāsrūrdhaṃ kṣīyamāṇadhātvindriyavalavīryotsāho 'nyahani
                        valīpalitakhālity akāsaśvāsaprabhṛtibhir upadravair abhibhūyamānaṃ
                        sarvvakriyāsvasamarthā jīrṇṇāgāram ivāvasīdati | tam vṛddham ācakṣate | </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.30">

                        mṛdusukumāropacitaśarīramanuṣyaprāyo vātakapharogabhūyiṣṭhaś cānūpaḥ ||
                            vakt<pc> </pc>ākāsam avitaralālpa<pc
                        > </pc>kaṇṭakavṛkṣavarṣaprasravaṇodapānaprāyoṣṇadārūṇavātapraviralālpaśailasthirakṛśaśarīramanuṣyaprāyo

                        <caesura/>

                <div corresp="1.36 in NAK 5-333" n="37" type="adhyāya">

                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 37 (<foreign xml:lang="sa"
                            >miśrakannāmādhyāyaṃ</foreign>) which is located between adhyāyas 35 and
                        36 in the Nepalese version, but is still numbered 37. Draft based on MS
                        H]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.37.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto miśrakannāmādhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.37.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mātuluṅgāgnimanthau ca bhadradāru mahauṣadhaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ahiṃsā caiva rāsnā ca pralepo vātaśophahā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.37.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dūrvvā ca nalamūlañ ca madhukañ candanan tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śītalāś ca gaṇāḥ sarvve pralepaḥ pittaśophahā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.37.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āgantuje raktaje ca lepa eṣo 'bhipūjitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidhirvviṣaghno viṣaje pittaghno 'bhihitas tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.37.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ajagandhāśvagandhā ca kālā śarala eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         eke ṣikājaśṛṅgī ca pralepaḥ śleṣmaśophahā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.37.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ete ca varggā lodhrañ ca pathyā piṇḍīkṛtāstuyaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         anantā ceti lepo 'yaṃ śophesarvvakṛtehitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.37.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snigdho 'mlalavaṇo vāte koṣṇaḥ śītaḥ payoyutaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pitte 'thoṣṇeh kaphe kṣāramūtrāḍhyastatpraśāntaye || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.9">

                        <caesura/>
                         śaṇaśigruphalātasī tilakalkāś ca sarṣaṣāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śaktavaḥ kiṇvamuṣṇāni dravyāṇyapi ca pācanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.37.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ciribilvāgniko dantī citrako hayamārakaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kapotakaṅkagṛddhrāṇām purīṣāṇi vidāraṇe || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.10ef">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.37.10ef</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣāradravyāṇi vā yāni kṣāro vā dāraṇaṃ paraṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.37.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dravyāṇām picchilānāṃ tu tvahyūlāni prapīḍanaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         yavagodhūmamāṣāṇāṃ cūrṇṇāni ca samāsataḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.12">

                        <caesura/>
                         śaṅkhinyaṃ koṭhasumanāḥkaravīraṃsuvarccalā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         śodhanāni kaṣāyāṇi varggaś cāragvadhādikaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.13">

                        <caesura/>
                         ajagandhājaśṛṅgī ca gavākṣī lāṅgalāhvayā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         pūtīkaś citrakaḥ pāṭhā viḍaṅgailāhareṇavaḥ | </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.14">

                        <caesura/>
                         kaṭutrikaṃ yavakṣāro lavaṇāni manaḥśilā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         kāśīsan tṛvṛtā dantī haritālaṃ surāṣṭrikā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.15">

                        <caesura/>
                         dravyeṣv eteṣu kurvvīta kalkān api ca śodhanān | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.16ab"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.37.17</label>

                        <caesura/>
                         jātīmūlaṃ haridre dve kāsīsaṃ kaṭurohiṇī | </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.16cd">

                        <caesura/>
                         pūrvvoddiṣṭeṣu cāṅgeṣu kuryāt saṃśodhanaṃ ghṛtaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.18ab"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.18cd">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.37.18cd</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mayūrako rājavṛkṣo nimbaḥ kośātakī tilā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.19">

                        <caesura/>
                         bṛhatī kaṇṭakārī ca haritālam manaḥśilā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         śodhanāni ca yāni syus taile yojyāni śodhane | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.37.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kāsīse saindhave kiṇve vacāyāṃ rajanīdvaye ||
                        <caesura/>
                         śodhanāṅgeṣu cānyeṣu cūrṇṇaṃ kurvvīta śodhanaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.21">

                         sālasārādisāreṣu paṭolatriphalāsu ca ||
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.22">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.23">

                        <caesura/>
                         śṛtaśīta kaṣāyam vā ropanārthe praśasyate | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.24">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.26">

                        <caesura/>
                         kākolyādiś ca yojyāḥ syuḥ praśastā ropaṇe ghṛte | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.27">

                        <caesura/>
                         priyaṅgavaś ca lodhrañ ca taile yojyāni ropaṇe | </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.28">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.37.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṅguka triphalā lodhraṃ kāśīsaṃ śravaṇāhvayā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         dhavośvakarṇṇayos tvak ca ropaṇe cūrṇṇamiṣyate | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.29"/>

                        <caesura/>

                        /></l>

                <div corresp="1.37 in NAK 5-333" n="36" type="adhyāya">

                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 37 (bhūmipravibhāgavijñānīyam) of the Nepalese
                        version, adhyāya 36 in the vulgate. Draft based on MS H]</head>

                    <note>There are large differences between the Ācārya 1931 and 1938 editions
                        version of Cakrapāṇidatta's commentary on this adhyāya.</note>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.36.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto bhūmipravibhāgavijñānīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.36.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svabhraśarkkarāśmaviṣamavalmīkaśmaśānāghatadevatāyatanasikatoṣairar
                        anupahatāmanūṣarāmabhaṃgurāmadūrodakāṃ snigdhāṃ prarohavatīṃ mṛdvīṃ sthirāṃ
                        samāṃ gaurīṃ lohitāṃ vā bhūmim auṣadha grahaṇāya parīkṣeta || tasyāṅ jātam
                        api hi krimaviṣaśastrātapapavanadahanatoyasambādhamārggair
                        anupahatamekasāraṃ puṣṭam avagāḍhamūlaṃ cauṣadhamādadyād ity eṣāṃ
                        bhūmiparīkṣāvibhāgaḥ sāmānyaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.36.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viśeṣatas tu tatra aśmavatī sthirā gurvvī śdhāmā kṛṣṇā vā
                        sthūlatṛṇaśasyaprāyāḥ svaguṇabhūyiṣṭhā | snigdhā śītalāsannodakā
                        snigdhatṛṇaśasyākomalavṛkṣaprāyā śuklāmbuguṇabhūyiṣṭhā || nānāvarṇṇā
                        laghvāśmavatī viralālyapāṇḍuraprarohāgniguṇabhūyiṣṭhā || rūkṣā
                        bhasmarāsabhavarṇṇā kṣatanuvṛkṣakoṭarālparasaprāyānilaguṇabhūyiṣṭhā || mṛdvī
                        samāvyabhravatyavyaktarasajalā mahāparvvatavṛkṣaprāryā syāmā
                        cākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.36.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra kecid ācāryāḥ prāvṛṭvarṣāśaraddhemantavasantagrīṣmeṣu yathāsaṃkhyam
                        mūlapattratvacakṣīrasāraphalāny ādadīta || tat tu na samyak kasmāt
                        saumyāgneyatvāj jagataḥ | saumyāny auṣadhāni saumyeṣv ṛtuṣv ādadīta |
                        āgneyāny āgneyeṣv evam avyāpannāni bhavanti || saumyāny auṣadhāni saumyeṣv
                        ṛtuṣu gṛhītāni somaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ bhūmau
                        madhuratarāsnigdhatarāṇiśītatarāṇi bhavanti | āgneyāny auṣadhāni āgneyeṣv
                        ṛtuṣu gṛhītānyagniguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ bhūmau uṣṇatarāṇi kaṭutarāṇi rūkṣatarāṇi
                        bhavanti | </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.36.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrā pṛthivῑguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ bhūmau jātāni virecanadravyāṇyādadīta |
                        agnyanilaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāñ ca vamanadravyāṇi | ubhayaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyām
                        ubhayatobhāgaharāṇi | ākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ saṃśamanāny evam balavattarāṇi
                        bhavanti | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.36.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvvāṇi cābhinavānyatra madhughṛtapippalīviḍaṅgebhya iti || </l>

                    <l corresp="1.36.11 of 1938 ed" xml:id="SS.1.36.9"/>
                    <l corresp="1.36.12 of 1938 ed" xml:id="SS.1.36.10"/>
                    <l corresp="1.36.13 of 1938 ed" xml:id="SS.1.36.11"/>
                    <l corresp="1.36.14 of 1938 ed" xml:id="SS.1.36.12"/>
                    <l corresp="1.36.15 of 1938 ed" xml:id="SS.1.36.13"/>


                    <l corresp="1.36.8 of 1938 ed" xml:id="SS.1.36.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.36.14" corresp="1.36.8 of 1938 ed</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viḍaṅga pippalī kṣaudraṃ sarpiś cāpyanavaṃ hitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śeṣam anyat tv abhinavaṃ gṛhṇīyād doṣavarjjitaṃ || </l>

                    <l corresp="1.36.16 of 1938 ed" xml:id="SS.1.36.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.36.15" corresp="1.36.16 of 1938 ed</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         jaṅgamānāṃ vayaḥsthānāñ carmaromanakhādikaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīramūtrapurīṣāṇi jīrṇṇāhāreṣu saṃharet || </l>

                    <l corresp="1.36.17 of 1938 ed" xml:id="SS.1.36.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.36.16" corresp="1.36.17 of 1938 ed</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         plotamṛdbhāṇḍaphalakaṃ saṅkuvinyastabheṣajān |
                        <caesura/>
                         praśastāyān diśi śucau bheṣajāgāram iṣyate || </l>

                    <l corresp="1.36.10 of 1938 ed" xml:id="SS.1.36.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.36.8" corresp="1.36.10 of 1938 ed</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gopālās tāpasā vyādhā ye cānye vanacāriṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūlāhārāś ca ye teṣāṃ bheṣajavyaktir iṣyate iti || </l>
                </div>

                <div n="38" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 38, draft based on MS H]</head>





                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.38.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto dravyasaṅgrahaṇīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.38.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pañcatriṃśad dravyagaṇā bhavanti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.38.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tad yathā | vidārigandhā vidārīviśvadevā sahadevāśvadaṃṣṭrā pṛthakparṇṇī
                        śatāvarīe śārivā jīvakarṣabho kṣudrasahā bṛhatyau
                        punarnnaiveraṇḍahaṃsapādīvṛścikālyṛṣabhī śṛgālavinnā ceti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.38.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vidārigandhādirayaṅ gaṇaḥ pittānilāpahaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śophagulmāṅgamarddorddhvaśvāsakāsavināśanaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.38.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āragvadhamadanaphalagopaghoṇṭākaṇṭakī
                        kaṇṭakārīkuṭajaphalapāṭhāpāṭalīmūrvvāsaptaparṇṇanimbakuraṇaaṭakaguḍūcīcitrakaśārṅgaṣṭādvikarañjapaṭolakirātatiktakāḥ
                        suṣavī ceti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.38.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āragvadhādirity eṣa gaṇaḥ śleṣmaviṣāpahaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mehakuṣṭajvaravamīkaṇḍūghno vraṇaśodhanaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.8"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.9"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.10"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.11"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.12">śālasārājakarṇṇakhadirakramubhūrjjameṣaśṛṅgīti
                        nisacandanakucandanaśiṃśapā śirīṣāsanadhavārjjunanaktamālapūtīkāś ca
                        karṇṇagurūṇi kālīyakañ ceti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.38.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śālasārādir ity eṣa gaṇaḥ kuṣṭhavināśanaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mehapāṇḍvāmayaharaḥ kaphamedoviśoṣaṇaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.13.1">
                        varuṇārttagalamadhuśigrutarkkārīmeṣaśṛṅgīpūtīkanaktamālapāṭalāgnimanthaśairīyakadvayaṃ
                        bimbīcitraśatāvarībilvājaśṛṅgīdarbbhābṛhatīdvayañ ceti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.13.2">
                        <label>1.38.13.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         varuṇādigaṇopyeṣa kaphamedo viśoṣaṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vinihanti śiraḥ śūlaṃ gulmābhyantaravidradhīḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.13.3">
                        <label>1.38.13.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vīratarasahacaradvayasairīyakadarbbhavṛkṣādanīgundrānalakuśakāśāśmabhedakāgni
                        manthamoraṭavasukavisarabhallūkakurūṭikendīvarakapotavaṅkāśvadaṃṣṭrā ceti
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.13.4">
                        <label>1.38.13.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vīratarādirity eṣa gaṇo vātavikārahṛt |
                        <caesura/>
                         śarkkarāśmarihāmūtrakṛcchrāghātarujāpahaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.38.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         lodhraśāvaralodhrapalāśakuṭannaṭāśokakaṭphalailavāluśallakījiṅjiṇīka
                        dambākadalī ceti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.38.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         eṣa lodhrādiko nāmnā medaḥ kaphaharogaṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yonidoṣaharastambhī vaṇyo viṣavināśanaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.38.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         arkkālarkkakarañjadvayanāgadantīmayūrakabhārggīrāsnendrapuṣpīkṣudrasvetābhallūkamahāsvetāvṛścikālyā
                        lavaṇātāpasavṛkṣaś ceti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.38.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         arkkādis tu gaṇo hyeṣa kaphamedoviṣāpahaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         krimikuṣṭhapraśamano viśeṣād vraṇaśodhanaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.38.19</label>
                        <caesura/>

                <div n="39" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 39, draft based on MS H]</head>




                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.39.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athātaḥ saṃśodhanasaṃśamanīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.39.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         madanakuṭajajīmūtakekṣvākudhāmārggavakṛtavedhanalodhrasarṣapaviḍaṅgapippalīkarañjaprapūnāḍakovidārāriṣṭāśvagandhāvidulabandhumadhukajīvantī
                        bimbīphalāmṛgervvāru citrasvetā śalapuṣpīvacācetyūrddhvabhāgaharāṇi || tatra
                        kovidārapūrvvāṇāmphalāni | kovidārādīnām mūlāni ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.39.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tṛvṛcchyāmādantīdravantīsaphalāviṣāṇigavākṣīcchagalāntrīpīlusnehāsuvarṇṇakṣīrīcitrakakiṇihīkuśakāsatilvakampilyakarampakapāṭalā
                        pūgaharītakyāmalakavibhītakanīlinīpañcaṅgulapūtīkāragvadhamahāvṛkṣasaptacchadārkkareṇu
                        jyotiṣmatī cetyadhobhāgaharāṇi ||tatra tilvakapūrvvāṇāṃ mūlāni |
                        tilvakādīnām pāṭalyantānāñ ca tvacaḥ | pūgādīnām eraṇḍāntānām phalāni |
                        pūtīkāragvadhayoḥ patrāṇi | śeṣāṇāṃ kṣīrāṇīti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.39.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kośātakī saptalā devadālī karavallikā cety ubhayato bhāgaharāṇi | eṣāṃ
                        svarasāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.39.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pippalīviḍaṅgāpāmārggaśigruśirīṣasiddhārthakamaricakaravīrabimbīgirikarṇṇikākiṇihīvacājyotiṣmatīkarañjārkkalaśunātiviṣāśṛ
                        ṅgaveratālīsatamālasurasārjjakeṅgudīmeṣaśṛṅgīmātuluṅgīmuruṅgīpīlujātīsālatālamadhūkalākṣāhiṃgulavaṇamadyagośakṛdrasomūtrāṇi
                        śirovirecanāni | tatra karavīrapūrvvāṇām phalāni | tālīsapūrvvāṇāṅ kandāḥ |
                        tālīsakādīnāmarjjakāntānām patrāṇi | iṅgudīmeṣaśṛṅgyos tvak |
                        mātuluṅgīmuruṅgīpīlujātīnām puṣpāṇi | śālatālamadhūkānāṃ sārāḥ | lākṣāhiṃgu
                        ca niryāsau | lavaṇāni pārthivaviśeṣāḥ | madyam āsutasaṃyogāḥ |
                        śakṛdrasamūtre malāviti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.39.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃśamanāni ata urdhvvam vakṣyāmaḥ || tatra
                        bhadradārukuṣṭhaharidrāvaruṇameṣaśṛṅgībalātibalārttagalakacchurāśallakīkuberākṣīvīratarasahacarāgnimanthavatsādanīśva
                        daṃṣṭrāśmabhedakārkkālarkkaśatāvarīpunarnnavāsukavasirakāñcanabhārggīvṛścikālīvadarayavakulattaprabhṛtīni
                        dve cādye pañcamūlyau samāsena vātasaṃ śamano varggaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.39.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         candanahrīverośīramañjiṣṭhāpayasyāgundraśevālakahlārakotpalamūrvvāprabhṛtīni
                        nyagrodhādirutpalādiriti samāsena pittasaṃśamano vargaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.39.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kāleyakāgurutailaparṇṇikākuṣṭhaharidrāśītaśivāśatapuṣpāsaralārāsnāprakīryodakīceṅgudīsumanāḥ
                        kākādanīlāṅgalakīhastiparṇṇamuñjālalāmajja
                        kaprabhṛtīnivallīkaṇṭakapañcamūlyau dve pippalyādir mmuṣkakādir vvacādiḥ
                        surasādirāragvadhādir utpalādir iti samāsena śleṣmasaṃśamano varggaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.39.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra sarvvāṇy evauṣadhāni vyādhagnipuruṣabalānyevekṣya vidadhyād
                        vyādhyabalād adhikam auṣadham upayuktan tam upasāmyavyādhim anyamāvahati ||
                        agnyabalād adhikam ajīrṇṇam viṣṭabhya vā pacyate | puruṣabalād adhikaṃ
                        glānimūrcchanā vahati | śamanam evaṃ saṃśodhanam atipātayati | hīnam ebhyo
                        dattam akiñcitkaram bhavati | tasmāt samam eva vidhyāt ||</l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.39.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavati cātra ||
                        <caesura/>
                         roge śodhanasādhye tu yam vidyād doṣam ulvanaṃ
                        <caesura/>
                         taṃ samīkṣya bhiṣak kuryād doṣapacyāvanaṃ mṛduḥ ||</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.11.1">
                        <label>1.39.11.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         jaloddhṛtauṣadhapalas toyadvikuḍavāyutaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pādāvaśeṣitaḥ kvāthaḥ pūtaḥ pānāya śasyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.11.2">
                        <label>1.39.11.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tadvat kṣīrārddhakuḍavaḥ sauṣadhastriguṇodakaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         kalkākṣamātrikaś cūrṇṇo biḍālapadakānvitaḥ ||<anchor n="SS.1.39.11.2-n1"
                        /></l>

                <div n="40" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 40, draft based on MS H]</head>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.40.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto dravyarasavīryavipākavijñānīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.2"/>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.40.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kecid ācāryā vruvate | dravyam pradhānam kasmāt vyavasthitatvāt | iha khalu
                        dravyam vyavasthitan na rasādayaḥ | yathā ye phale rasādayas te pakve na
                        bhavanti || nityatvāc ca nityaṃ hi dravyam anityaṃ hi guṇāḥ | yathā kalkādi
                        pravibhāgās tad eva sampannarasagandhaṃ vyāpannarasagandhavān bhavatīti |
                        svajātivyavasthānāc ca yathā pārthivaṃ dravyam anyabhāvan na gacchati | evaṃ
                        śoṣāṇi | pañcendriyagrahaṇāc ca | pañcaindriyair gṛhyate draṣṭavyan na
                        rasādayaḥ | āśrayatvāc ca dravyam āśritārasā iti | ārambha sāmarthyāc ca
                        dravyāśrita ārambhaḥ || yathā vidārigandhādim āhṛtyāv adya vipaced ity evam
                        ādiṣu na rasādiṣ ārambhaḥ | śāstraprāmāṇyāc ca śāstraṃ ha | dvividhan
                        dravyaṃ sthāvarañ jañgam ti | kramāpekṣikatvāc ca rasādīnāṃ rasādayo hi
                        dravyakramam apekṣante yathā taruṇe taruṇāḥ | saṃpūrṇa sampūrṇā iti |
                        ekadeśasādhyatvāc ca dravyāṇām ekadeśenāpi vyādhayaḥ sādhyante | yathā
                        mahāvṛkṣakṣīreṇeti | tasmād dravyam pradhānan rasādayaḥ kasmāt
                        niravayavatvāt dravyasya | dravyalakṣaṇan tu kriyāguṇasamavāyaḥ kriyādravye
                        vidyate | guṇāḥ samavāyakāraṇañ ceti ||</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.40.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nety āhur anye rasās tu pradhānan kasmāt āgamāt āgamo hi śāstram ity ucyate
                        | śāstre rasā adhikṛtā yathā rasāyatta āhāra iti | upadeśāc ca | upadiśyate
                        hi | yathā madhurāmlalavaṇā vātaṃ śamayanti | ato rasāḥ pradhānaṃ | anumāc
                        ca | rasato hy anumīyate dravyaṃ | yathā madhuram iti || ṛṣivacanāc ca |
                        ṛṣivacano vedaḥ | yathā kiñcid ījyārtham madhuram āhared iti | tasmāt rasāḥ
                        pradhānaṃ | raseṣu tu guṇasaṃjñā rasalakṣaṇam atropadekṣyāmaḥ | </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.40.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nety āhur anye vīryam pradhānam iti | kasmāt prādhānyāt |
                        ihatvauṣadhakarmmāṇi vīrya prādhānyaṃ na bhavanti | tad yathā |
                        urddhabhāgodhobhāgobhayabhāgasaṃśamanaṃ
                        sāṅgrāhikadīpanalekhanavṛṃhaṇarasāyanavājīkaraṇaś ca
                        yathuharavilayanadāraṇamarddanaprāṇaghnaviṣapraśamanāni vīrya prādhānyena
                        bhavanti | tantu vīryaṃ dvividhaṃ | uṣṇaṃ śītaṃ cāgniṣomīyatvāj jagataḥ |
                        kecid aṣṭavidham āhuḥ | uṣṇaṃ śītaṃ snigdhaṃ rūkṣam vi ṣadam piccilam mṛdus
                        tīkṣṇañ ceti | etāni khalu vīryāṇi svabhāvaguṇotkarṣād rasam
                        abhibhūyātmakarmma kurvvanti | yathā tāvad vṛhatyañ ca mūlaṅ kaṣāya tiktaṃ
                        vātaṃ śamayaty uṣṇavīryatvāt | kaṭukā pippalīpittaṃ śamayati |
                        mṛduśītavīryatvāt | tiktā kākamācī pittaṃ varddhayaty uṣṇavīryatvāt |
                        kaṭukaṃ mūlaṃ śleṣmāṇaṃ varddhayati snigdhavīryatvāt | amlaṃ kapitthaṃ
                        śleṣmāṇaṃ ti rukṣavīryatvāt || bha || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.40.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ye rasā vātaśamanā bhavanti yadi teṣu vai |
                        <caesura/>
                         rukṣalāghavaśaity āni na te hanyuḥ samīraṇam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.40.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ye rasāḥ pittaśamanā bhavanti yadi teṣuvai |
                        <caesura/>
                         taikṣṇyauṣṇyalaghutā caiva na te talkarmmakāriṇaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.40.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ye rasāḥ śleṣmaśamanā bhavanti yadi teṣu vai |
                        <caesura/>
                         snehagauravaśaity ānu na te tatkarmmakāriṇaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.40.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmād vīryaṃ pradhānam iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.40.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nety āhur anye vipākaḥ pradhānam iti | kasmāt samyaṅ mithyā vipakvatvāt |
                        iha hi dravyāṇyapaha tāni samyaṅ mithyā cāvipakvāni guṇan doṣam vā janayaṃti
                        | tatrāhur anye prati ra sampāka iti | vipākaḥ kecit trividham icchanti |
                        madhuram amlam kaṭukañceti | tat tu na samyak | bhūtaguṇād āgamāc cāmlo
                        vipāko nāsti | pittaṃ hi vidagdham amlatām upaity āgneyatvāt | yad evaṃ
                        lavaṇo 'pyanyaḥ pāke bhaviṣyati | śleṣmā hi vidagdho lavaṇatām upaiti |
                        tamādasiddhānta eṣaḥ | pratirasam amlāmlasyaivaṃ sarvvaṣām iti dṛṣṭāntañ
                        codāharanti | yathā śāliyavamudgādayaḥ prakīrṇāḥ svabhāvam uttarakāle pi na
                        parity ajanti tadvat iti | kecit punar avalavanto valavatāṃ vaśamāyānt it
                        evam avasthitaḥ pāka iti | āgame svāha | dvividha eva pāko madhuraḥ kaṭukaś
                        ca | tayor madhurākhyo guruḥ kaṭukākhyo laghur iti | tatra
                        pṛthivyaptejovāyvākāśānāṃ dvaividhyam bhavati | guṇasādharmyān gurutā |
                        laghutā ca pṛthivyā yo gurvyaḥ | śeṣāṇi laghūni tasmād dvividha eva pāko
                        bhavati || bha ||</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.40.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dravyeṣu pacyamāneṣu yeṣv ambupṛthivīguṇāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nivarttante 'dhikās tatra pāko madhura ucyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.12">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.13">

                        <caesura/>
                         pṛthak tvavādināmeṣeva vādinām vādasaṃgrahaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         caturṇṇām api sāmagryam icchantyatra vipaścitaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.40.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tad dravyam ātmanā kiñcit kiñcid vīryeṇa sevitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kiñcid rasavipākābhyān doṣaṃ hanti karoti vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.15">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.16">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.17">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         raseṣu na bhavantyete nirguṇāḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.18">

                        <caesura/>
                         dravye dravye ca yasmāddhi vipacyante na ṣaḍ rasāḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.19">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.20">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.21">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.41.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto dravyaviśeṣavijñānīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.41.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra pṛthivyaptejovāyvākāśānāṃ samudāyād dravyābhinirvṛttir bbhavati |
                        idaṃ pārthivam idam apyam idan tejasam idam vāyavyam idam ākāśyam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.1">
                        <label>1.41.4.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra sthūla<pc> </pc>sāndra<pc> </pc>manda<pc> </pc>sthira<pc
                            > </pc>guru<pc> </pc>kaṭhina<pc> </pc>gaṃdha<pc> </pc>guṇa<pc
                        > </pc>bahulam īṣatkaṣāyaprāyaso madhuram iti pārthivan tat
                            sthairya<pc> </pc>gaurava<pc> </pc>saṃghātopacaya<pc> </pc>karaṃ
                        viśeṣataś cādhogatisvabhāvam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.2">
                        <label>1.41.4.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śīta<pc> </pc>stimita<pc> </pc>manda<pc> </pc>guru<pc> </pc>rasa<pc> </pc>sāndra<pc> </pc>mṛdu<pc> </pc>picchila<pc> </pc>rasa<pc> </pc>guṇa<pc> </pc>bahulam
                        īṣadamlaṃ prāyaso madhuram āpyan tat snehanahlādanaviṣyandanakaram iti | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.3">
                        <label>1.41.4.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tīkṣṇoṣṇarūkṣasūkṣmalaghuviṣadaṃ rūpaguṇabahulam īṣadamlaprāyam viśeṣataś
                        corddhvagatisvabhāvam iti taijasaṃ ||
                        taddahanapacanatāpanaprakāśanaprabhāvarṇṇakaram iti | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.4">
                        <label>1.41.4.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sūkṣmarūkṣakharaśiśiralaghuviṣadaṃ sparśaguṇabahulam īṣattiktam viśeṣataḥ
                        kaṣāyam iti vāyavyaṃ tadvaiṣadyaṃ lāghavaglapanavirūkṣaṇakaram iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.5">
                        <label>1.41.4.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ślakṣṇasūkṣmavyavāyiviṣadaviviktarasaṃ śabdaguṇabahulam ākāśyan tasmāt tat
                        mārddavasauṣiryalāghavakaram iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.41.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         anena nidarśanena nānauṣadhabhūtañ jagati kiñcid dravyam astīti kṛtvā tan
                        taṃ yuktiviśeṣamarthañ cābhipratītya svavīryaguṇayuktāni dravyāṇi
                            kārmmukāni<anchor n="SS.1.41.5-n1"/> bhavanti || tāni yadā kurvvanti sa
                        kālaḥ | yat kurvanti tat karmma | yena kurvvanti tad vīryaṃ | yatra
                        kurvvanti tad adhikaraṇaṃ | yathā kurvvanti sa upāyaḥ | yad abhiniṣpādayanti
                        tat phalam iti | </l>

                    <ab corresp="#SS.1.41.5" type="apparatus">
                        <list type="notes">
                            <item corresp="#SS.1.41.5-n1">The word <foreign>kārmuka</foreign> is
                                known in early medical texts from this instance and one in the
                                    <title>Carakasaṃhitā</title> 1.26.13. The word is formed by
                                P.5.1.103 in the sense “capable of accomplishing an action."</item>
                        </list>
                    </ab>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.41.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tad atra virecanadravyāṇy ambupṛthivīguṇabhūyiṣṭhāni | pṛthivyāpo hi
                        gurvvyaḥ | gurutvād adho gacchanti | tasmād virecanadravyāṇy
                        ambupṛthivīguṇabhūyiṣṭhāni | vamanadravyāṇy agnivāyuguṇabhūyiṣṭhāni |
                        agnivāyū hi laghū laghutvāc corddhvam uttiṣṭhataḥ | tasmād vamanaprāmāṇyād
                        agnivāyubhūyiṣṭhāny ubhayaguṇabhūyiṣṭhan dravyam ubhayato bhāgaharaṃ |
                        ākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ saṃśamanaṃ | sāṃgrāhikam anilaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ | dīpanam
                        agniguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ | lekhanam anilānalaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ | bṛṃhanam
                        pṛthivyambuguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ | evam auṣadhakarmmāṇy anumānāt sādhayet || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.41.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanti ślokāḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         mahyambvagnyātmakair ddravyais tribhiḥ sāmyati mārutaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         khabhūmyambuvāyujaiḥ pittañ caturbbhiḥ saṃpraśāmyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.41.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphaḥ khatejo'nilajais tribhiḥ śāmyati dehināṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         khavāyuktābhyān dravyābhyāṃ vṛddhim abhyeti mārutaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.41.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āgneyam eva yad dravyan tena pittam udīryate |
                        <caesura/>
                         mahyambujābhyān dravyābhyāṅ kaphaś cābhivivarddhate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.41.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         evam eva guṇādhikyaṃ dravye dravye vyavasthitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dviśo vā bahuśo vāpi jñātvā doṣe 'vacācaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.41.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra ya ime guṇāṣṭauvīryasaṃjñakāḥ |
                        śītoṣṇasnigdharūkṣamṛdutīkṣṇapicchilaviṣadās teṣān tīkṣṇoṣṇāv āgneyau |
                        śītapicchilāv ambuguṇabhūyiṣṭhau | pṛthivīsomaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaḥ | snehas
                        toyākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ | mṛdutvaṃ | vāyuguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ raukṣyaṃ |
                        kṣitisamīraṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ vaiṣadyaṃ | vipākāv uktaguṇau | karmmāṇy uṣṇasya
                        dahanapācanamūrcchanasvedanavamanavirecanāni || śītasya
                        prahlādanaviṣkambhanasthirīkaraṇaprasādanakledanajīvanāni | snigdhasya
                        snehanabṛṃhaṇasantarppaṇavyājīkaraṇavayaḥsthāpanāni ||
                        rūkṣasyānilavṛddhisaṃgrahaṇapīḍanavirūkṣaśoṣarohaṇāni || viṣadasya
                        kledāvūṣaṇavirūkṣaśoṣarohaṇāni ||
                        picchilasyopalepanapūraṇabṛṃhaṇasaṃśleṣaṇavyājīkaraṇāni || mṛdo raktamān
                        saprasādanamukhyasaṃsparśanāni || tīkṣṇasya saṅgrahācūṣaṇāvadāraṇaśrāvaṇāni
                        | tatroṣṇasnigdhau vātaghnau | śītamṛdupicchilāḥ pittaghnāḥ |
                        tīkṣṇarūkṣaviṣadāḥ śleṣmaghnāḥ | gurupāko vātapittaghnaḥ | laghupākaḥ
                        śleṣmapittaghna iti | teṣu mṛduśītoṣṇāḥ sparśagrāhyāḥ | picchilaviṣadau
                        cakṣuḥsparśābhyāṃ | snigdharūkṣau cakṣuṣā | tīkṣṇaḥ sukhaduḥkhotpādanāt |
                        gurupākaḥ sṛṣṭaviṇmūtratayā kaphāṃ kleśanañ ca | laghur bbaddhaviṇmūtratayā
                        mārutakopanañ ca | tatra tulyaguṇeṣu bhūteṣu rasavaiśeṣyam upalakṣayet ||
                        yathā madhuro guruś ca pārthivaḥ | madhurasnigdhaśītāś cāpyā iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.41.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         || bhavati cātra || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.12i">
                        <label>1.41.12i</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         guṇā ye uktā dravyeṣu śarīreṣv api tān viduḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sthānavṛddhikṣayāt tasmād dehināṃ dravyahetukā iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.trailer"> || 41 ||</l>

                </div>


                <div n="42" type="adhyāya">

                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 42, draft based on MS H]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.42.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto rasaviśeṣavi-jñānīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.42.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ākāśapavanadahanatoyabhūmiṣu yathāsaṅkhyam ekottaraparivṛddhāḥ || śa
                        bdasparśarūparasagandhāḥ || tasmād āpyo rasaḥ parasparānupraveśāc ca
                        sarvveṣāṃ sānnidhyam asti utkarṣāt tu grahaṇaṃ | sa khalvāpyo rasaḥ
                        śeṣabhūtasaṃsarggādvidagdhaḥ ṣaḍvidho bhavati | tad yathā | madhuro 'mlo
                        lavaṇaḥ kaṭukastiktaḥ kaṣāya iti | tatrodakavāhulyātmadhuraḥ |
                        toyāgnivāhulyādamlaḥ bhūmyagnivāhulyāl lavaṇaḥ vāyvākāśavāhulyāttiktaḥ |
                        vāyvagnivāhulyātkaṭukaḥ pṛthivyanilavāhulyātkaṣāya iti || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.42.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra madhurāmlalavaṇā vātaghnāḥ | madhuratiktakaṣāyāḥ pittaghnāḥ
                        kaṭutiktakaṣāyāḥ śleṣmaghnāḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.42.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra vāyurātmaivātmā | pittamāgneyaṃ | śleṣma saumya iti || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.42.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ta ete rasāḥ svayonivardhanā anyayonipraśamanāś ca | </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.42.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kecid āhur agnīṣomīyatvājjagataḥ | dvividhā rasāḥ saumyā āgneyāś ca | tatra
                        madhuratiktakaṣāyāḥ saumyāḥ dvividhā kaṭvamlalavaṇā āgneyāḥ |
                        madhurāmlalavaṇāḥ snigdhā guravaś ca dvividhā kaṭutiktakaṣāyā rūkṣā laghavaś
                        ca | saumyāḥ śītāḥ | āgneyās tūṣṇāḥ | </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.8.1">
                        <label>1.42.8.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra śaityarūkṣalāghavavaiṣadyaguṇalakṣaṇo vāyuḥ | tasya samānayoniḥ
                        kaṣāyo rasaḥ | saumyaḥ śaityāc chaity am abhivardhayati | raukṣyād raukṣyaṃ
                        lāghavāl lāghavaṃ vaiṣadyād vaiṣadyam iti || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.8.2">
                        <label>1.42.8.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         auṣṇyataikṣṇyaraukṣyalāghavavaiṣadyaguṇalakṣaṇampittantasya samānayoniḥ
                        kaṭuko rasaḥ | saumya auṣṇyād auṣṇyam abhivardhayati | taikṣṇyāt taikṣṇyaṃ
                        raukṣyād raukṣyaṃ lāghavāl lāghavaṃ vaiśadyād vaiśadyam iti || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.8.3">
                        <label>1.42.8.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mādhuryasnehagauravaśaityapaicchilyaguṇalakṣaṇaḥ śleṣmā tasya samānayo
                        nirmadhuro rasaḥ | saumya mādhuryāt mādhuryam abhivardhayati | snehāt snehaṃ
                        gauravād gauravaṃ śaityāc chaityaṃ paicchilyāt paicchilyam iti ||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.42.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya punar vviparītaḥ kaṭuko rasaḥ | śleṣmaṇaḥ pratyanīkatvāt |
                        kaṭukyātmādhuryam abhibhavati | raukṣyāt snehaṃ lāghavād gauravaṃ auṣṇyāt
                        paicchity an tad etan nidarśanamātram uktaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.42.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rasalakṣaṇam ata ūrdhvaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ || tatra yaḥ paritoṣam utpādayati
                        tarppayati mukhopalepañ janayati prahlādayati śleṣmāṇañ cābhivardhayati sa
                        madhuraḥ || yo dantaharṣam utpādayati | mukhāśrāvañ jana-yati śraddhāñ
                        cotpādayati so 'mlaḥ || yo bhaktarucim utpādayati | kaphaprasekañ janayati
                        mārddavañ copādayati sa lavaṇaḥ || yo jihvām udvejayati śiro gṛhṇāti nāsikāñ
                        ca śrāvayati sa kaṭukaḥ || yo gale śoṣam utpāda-yati mukhavaiṣadyam
                        utpādayati bhaktaruciñ copādyati sa tiktaḥ || ya āsyam pariśoṣayati- jihvāṃ
                        stambhayati kaṇṭham badhnāti hṛdayam pīḍayati sa kaṣāyaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.1">
                        <label>1.42.10.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rasaguṇān ata ūrdhvam vakṣyāmaḥ || tatra madhuro raso raktamāṃsado
                        'sthimajjojaḥ śukravardhanaś cākṣuṣyaḥ keśyauvalakṛtsandhānaḥ śoṇitaḥ
                        śoṇitaprasādo vālavṛddhakṣatakṣīṇahitaḥ ṣaṭpadapipīlikānāmiṣṭatamaḥ ||
                        tṛṣṇāmūrcchādāhaḥ praśamanaḥ | ṣaḍindriyaprasādanaś ceti | sa evaṃguṇo 'py
                        eka evātyartham upayujyamānaḥ kāsaḥ śvāso
                        lasakavamathurvvadanamādhuryasvaropaghātakṛmigalagaṇḍān āpādayati |
                        tathārvvudaślīpadabastigudopalepābhiṣyandaprabhṛtīn nayanavikārānn upajayati
                        || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.2">
                        <label>1.42.10.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         amlas tu jaraṇaḥ pācanapavananigrahaṇo nulomano vidāhī vahiḥśītaḥ kledanaḥ
                        prāyaśo hṛdyaś ceti | sa khalv evaṃguṇo 'py eka evātyartham upayujyamāno
                        dantaharṣanayanasammīlanaromasamvejanakaphavilāyanaśarīrapraśithilatām
                        āpādayati | tathā
                        kṣatavihatadagdhadaṣṭabhagnaśū-nacyutāvamathitacchiyavisarppitacchinnaviddhotpiṣṭādīni
                        pāca-yaty āgneyasvabhāvatvvāt || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.3">
                        <label>1.42.10.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         lavaṇas tu saṃśodhanaḥ pācano viśleṣaṇas tarppaṇaḥ kledanaḥ śaithilyakṛt
                        sarvvarasapratyanīkabhūto mārggaviśodhanaḥ sarvvaśarīrāvayavamārddavakaraś
                        ceti | sa khalu evaṃguṇo 'py eka evātyartham upasevyamāno gātrakaṇḍūko tha
                        śophavaivarṇṇakaraḥ svaropaghātendriyopatāpān upajanayati |
                        tathākṣimukhapākaraktapittavātaśoṇitāmlīkāprabhṛtīnvikārān upajanayati || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.4">
                        <label>1.42.10.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṭukas tu dīpanaḥ pācano rocanaḥ śodhanaḥ sthaulyā
                        lyālasakaviṣakuṣṭhakaṇḍūpraśamanaḥ sandhibandhacchedano vasādanas
                        stanyaśukrakaphamedasām upahantā ceti | sa khalv evaṃguṇo 'py eka
                        evātyartham upayujyamāno bhramamadagalatālvoṣṭhaśoṣadāhasantāpān āpādayati |
                        tathā valavighātakampatodabhedakṛt karacaraṇapārśvapṛṣṭhaprabhṛtiṣu ca
                        vātaśūlān upajanayati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.5">
                        <label>1.42.10.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tiktas tu rocano dīpanaḥ śodhanaḥ kaṇḍūkoṣṭhatṛṣṇāmūrcchāpraśanaḥ
                        stanyaśodhano viṇmūtrakledamedovasāpūyopaśoṣaṇaś ceti | sa khalv evaṅguṇo
                        'py eka evātyartham upayujyamāno gātramanyāstambhākṣepakordditaśiraḥśūlān
                        upa-janayati | tathā bhramatodabhedacchedāsyavairasyāny āpādayati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.6">
                        <label>1.42.10.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyas tu saṅgrāhiko ropaṇaḥ stambhanaḥ śodhanollekhanaḥ śoṣaṇaḥ pīḍanaḥ
                        kledopaśoṣaṇaś ceti | sa khalv evaṅguṇo 'py eka evātyartham upayujyamāno
                        hṛdayapīḍāsyaśoṣodarādhmānavākyagrahamanyāstambhaprabhṛtīn vikārān
                        upajanayati | tathā gātrasphuraṇacimicimāyanākuñcanākṣepaṇaprabhṛtīn
                        vikārānupajanayati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.42.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvveṣām eva dravyāṇy upadekṣyāmaḥ | tad yathā kākolyādi
                        kṣīraghṛtavasāmajjaśāliyavagodhūmamāṣaśṛṅgāṭakakaśeruka
                        kālāṅkālukapiyālapuṣkaravījakāśmaryamadhūkadrākṣākharjūrarājādananālikerekṣuvikārāḥ
                        | balātibalātmaguptāvidārīpayasyāgokṣurakakṣīramoraṭamadhūlikākūṣmāṇḍādiḥ
                        samāsena madhuro varggaḥ ||
                        dāḍimāmalakamātuluṅgāmrāmrātakakapitthakaramarddavadaraprācīnāmalakakośāmrabhavyapārāvatavetraphalatintiḍīkalajacāmlavetasadantaśaṭhadadhitakrasurāsauvīratuṣodakadhānyāmlaprabhṛtīni
                        samāsenāmlo varggaḥ ||
                        saindhavasauvarccalaviḍapākyaromakasāmudrapācimakṣāroṣarasuvarccilaprabhṛtīni
                        samāsena lavaṇo varggaḥ || pippa-lyādiḥ surasādir
                        mmadhuśigrumūlakalaśunasumukhaśītaśivakuṣṭhadevadāruhareṇukā
                        'valgujaphalacaṇḍāguggulumustalāṅgalakīśukanāsīpīluprabhṛtī-ni śālasārādiś
                        ca prāyaśaḥ kaṭuko varggaḥ ||
                        āragvadhādirgguḍūcyādirmmaṇḍūkaparṇṇīvetrakarīraharidrādvayendrayavavaruṇasvādukaṇṭakasaptaparṇṇavṛhatīdvayaśaṃkhinītṛvṛtkṛtavedhanakarkkoṭakakāravellavārttākukaravīrasumanāḥśaṃkhapuṣpyapāmārggatrāyamāṇāśokarohivaijayantīsuvarccalāvṛścikālījyotiṣmatīprabhṛtīni
                        tikto varggaḥ || nyagrodhādirambaṣṭhādir lodhrādiḥ priyaṅvādistriphalā
                        śallakījamvvasthitindukādīni katakaśākaphalāni sālasārādiś ca prāyasaḥ
                        kuravakakovidārajīvantīsuniṣaṇṇakaprabhṛtīni varakādayo mudgādayaś ca
                        samāsena kaṣā-yo varggaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.42.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatraiteṣāṃ rasānāṃ saṃyogās triṣaṣṭirv bhavanti || tad yathā pañcadaśa
                        dvikāḥ | viṃśatis trikāḥ | pañcadaśa catuṣkāḥ | ṣaṭ pañcakāḥ | ekaṣaṭkāḥ |
                        ekaikaśaś ca śaḍrasā iti | teṣām anyatra vakṣyāmaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.42.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavati cātra ||
                        <caesura/>
                         yuktāḥ ṣaḍadhigacchanti valino vaśyatāṃ rasāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā doṣāḥ prakupitā vaśaṃ yānti valīyasa iti ||</l>
