                <div n="43" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 43, draft based on MS H]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.43.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto vamanadravyavikalpavijñānīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.3.part1">
                        <label>1.43.3.part1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vamanadravyānām phalākhyānām madhye madanaphalāni śreṣṭhatamāni bhavanti ||
                        tatra madanapuṣpāṇām ātapaśuṣkāṇā cūrṇaprakuñcaṃ pratyak puṣpīnimvakaṣāyāṇām
                        anyatamenālo pāyayitvā vāmayet | madanaśatvāṭūcūrṇṇāny evam
                        madhulavaṇayuktāny abhiprataptāni | madanaśalāṭucūrṇṇasiddhām vā tilayavāgūn
                        | nivṛttām vā nātihariti pāṇḍūnāṃ kuśamūḍhāvavaddhamṛdgomayapraliptānāṃ
                        yavavūsamāṣaśālyādidhānyarāśāvaṣṭharātroṣitaklinnabhinnānām
                        phalapippalīrāhṛtyātape pariśoṣayet tāsāṃ dadhipalavimṛditapariśuṣkāṇāṃ
                        subhājanasthānām antarnnakhamuṣṭhim uṣṇena yaṣṭhīmadhukaṣāyeṇa
                        kovidārādhyanyatamakāṣāyeṇa vā vimṛdya trirātraparyuṣitam
                        madhusaindhavayuktam āśīrbhir abhimantritam udaṅmukhaḥ prāṅmukham āturam
                        pāyayet anena mantreṇa abhimantrya ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.3.1">
                        <label>1.43.3.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         brahmadakṣāśvirūdrendrabhūcandrārkkānilānalāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ṛṣayaḥ sauṣadhigrāmā bhūtasaṃghāś ca pāntu te ||<anchor n="SS.1.43.3.1-n1"
                        />
                    </l>
                    <ab corresp="#SS.1.43.3.1" type="apparatus">
                        <list type="Testimonia">
                            <item corresp="#SS.1.43.3.1-n1">This and the next passage are found in
                                the <title>Agnipurāṇa</title> 279.014cd (Mitra 1870: v.3,
                                p.35).</item>
                        </list>
                    </ab>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.3.2">
                        <label>1.43.3.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rasāyaneva siddhānān devānām amṛtaṃ yathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         sudhevottamanāgānāsbhaiṣajyam idam astu te ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.3.part2">
                        <label>1.43.3.part2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viśeṣeṇa śleṣmajvarapratiśyāyāntarvvidradhiṣv apravarttamāne doṣe
                        pippalīvacāsarṣapakalkonmiśrair uṣṇāmvubhiḥ punaḥ punaḥ pravarttayed āsamyag
                        vāntalakṣaṇād iti | madanaphalamajjacūrṇṇam vā tat kvāthaparibhāvitam vasena
                        dravyakaṣāyeṇa | madanaphalamajjā siddham vā payaḥ |
                        madanaphalamajjasiddhena vā payasā vā yavāgūm adhobhāgāsṛhṛdrogayoḥ |
                        madanaphalamajjasiddhasya vā payaso dadhibhāvam upagatasya | dadhyuttarakaṃ
                        dadhi vā kaphaprasekaśarddistameṣu | madanaphalamajjācūrṇṇa rasam vā
                        bhallātakasenhavadādāya phāṇitībhūtaṃ lehayet | ātapaśuṣkam vā jīvantī
                        kaṣāyeṇa pittakaphasthānagate | madanaphala majjākvātham vā pippalyādi
                        prativāpaṃ ūṣaṇanimvakaṣāya yor anyatamena santarppaṇaṃ |
                        kaphasarvvavyādhiharam iti madanaphalam uktaṃ | </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.43.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         jīmūtakakusumacūrṇṇam vā pūrvvavad eva kṣīreṇa nivṛtteṣu yavāgūṃ romaseṣu |
                        santānikām vā nirllomaśeṣu | dadhyuttarakaṃ haritakapāṇḍuṣu | dadhi tat
                        kaṣāyasaṃsṛṭāṃ surām vā paryāgateṣu | madanaphalamajja </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.43.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vidhānavat kuṭajaphalamajjavidhānaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.6"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.43.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ikṣvākukusumacūrṇṇam vā pūrvvavad eva kṣīreṇa | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.43.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dhāmārgavasyāpi madanaphalamajjā vidhānavad upayogaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.43.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛtavedhanamadanaphalamajjapippalīmām vamanadravyaparibhāvitānām bahuśaś
                        cūrṇṇam utpalādiṣu dattam āghrā ya vasati tattvanavavaddhadoṣeṣu
                        yavāgūmākaṇṭham pītavatsu ca dadyād iti | śirovirecanāny evaṃ pradhānatamāni
                        bhavanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.10"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.43.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavati cātra
                        <caesura/>
                         kalkaiḥ kaṣāyaiḥ svarasaiś ca cūrṇṇair api ca vuddhimān |
                        <caesura/>
                         peyalehyādibhojyeṣu vamanānyūpakalpayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.44.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto virecanadravyavikalpavijñānīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.44.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         aruṇābhan tṛvṛn mūlaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ mūlavirecane |
                        <caesura/>
                         pradhānas tilvakas tv akṣu phaleṣv api harītakī ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.44.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                        <caesura/>
                         snehāpayaḥ payassūktam iti prādhānyasaṅgrahaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         teṣām vidhānaṃ vakṣyāmi yathāvad anupūrvvaśaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.44.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vairecanadravyakaṣāyapītam mūlam
                        <caesura/>
                         mahattraivṛtamatra śuddhaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         cūrṇṇīkṛtaṃ saindhavanāgarāḍhyam
                        <caesura/>
                         pibet tad amlair anilādhijuṣṭaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.44.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svādukvāthair api cekṣor vvikāraiḥ paitteroge kṣīrayuktān nihanyāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         drākṣārasatriphalākvāthamūtrair yuktam pibet kaphajavyoṣagāḍhaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.44.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         trivarṇṇakatrikaṭukābhyānyuktaṃ lihyāc cūrṇṇan tadguḍenābhiyojyaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kvāthaprasthe kuḍavan tasya dadyāt yuktyā dadyān nāgaraṃ saindhavañ ca
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.44.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pacet sarvvaṃ yāvadetad ghanaṃ syāl lehībhūtan tatprayojyaṃ tatas tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         tṛvṛtkalkonāgarārddhena yuktaḥ sasaindhavo mūtrayuktastu peyaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.44.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sametṛvṛn nāgare cābhayāñ ca dadyād arddham pūgaphalaṃ sadāruḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viḍaṃgasāraṃ marica vaiṣayogaḥ sasaindhavo mūtrayuktaḥ pradhānaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.10"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.11"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.44.12</label>

                        <caesura/>
                         sumardditaṃ sarppiṣā tacchritena tatkvāthośmasveditā varttitañ ca ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.13">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                <div n="45" type="adhyāya">

                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 45, draft based on MS H]</head>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.45.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto dravadravyaviśeṣavijñānīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.2"/>

                    <!-- <lg type="varga"> -->

                    <p ana="subheading" style="bold">[Pānīyavarga]</p>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.45.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pānīyaṃm āntarīkṣyam anirddeśyarasam amṛtaṃ jīvanan tarppaṇan dhāraṇam
                        āśvāsajananaṃ śramaklamapipāsāmadamūrcchātandrāpraśamanam ekāntataḥ
                        pathyatamañ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.45.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tad evāvanau patitam anyatamam upalabhyate |
                        nadīsarastaḍāgakūpavāpīpraśravaṇodbhijacauṇṭyādiṣu sthāneṣv anyatamaṃ rasam
                        upabhate | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.45.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra lohitakapilapā-ṇḍupītanīlaśukleṣv avanipradeśeṣu
                        madhurāmlalavaṇakaṭutiktakaṣāyā yathāsaṃkhyam udakarasā bhavantīty eke
                        bhāṣante || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.45.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tat tu na samyak pṛthivyādīnām anyo 'nyānupraveśakṛtaḥ sa khalūdakaraso
                        bhavatyutkarṣāpakarṣakṛtena saṃyogaviśeṣeṇa || tatra
                        svalakṣaṇodakaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyām madhuraṃ | toyāgniguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyām amlaṃ|
                        pṛthivyagniguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ lavaṇaṃ | vāyvagniguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṅ kaṭukaṃ|
                        vāyvākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ tiktaṃ | pṛthivyanilaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṅ kaṣāyaṃ |
                        ākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyām avyaktarasam avyaktaṃ hy ākāśam ity atas tat pradhānam
                        avyaktarasatvāt tat peyam āntarīkṣālābhe | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.45.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrānta-rikṣañ caturvvidhaṃ || tadyāthā | dhāraṃ kāraṃ tauṣāraṃ haimam iti
                        | teṣān dhāraṃ pradhānaṃ laghutvāt tat punar dvividhaṃ | gāṅgaṃ sāmudrañ ca
                        tayoḥ parīkṣaṇaṃ | tatra śālyodanapiṇḍam akuthitam avidagdhaṃ |
                        rajatabhājanopahitaṃ varṣati deve kurvvīta sa cet muhūrttasthitas tādṛśa eva
                        bhavati | tad gāṅgam iti avagantavyaṃ | varṇṇānyatāsitthaprakledo vā
                        tatsāmudram iti vidyāt | tan nopādeyaṃ | sāmudram apy āśvayuji māsi gṛhītaṃ
                        gāṅgavad bhavati | tad upādeyam iti | śuklapaṭaikadeśapracyutam athavā
                        harmmyatalaparibhraṣṭam anyair vvā prayogair ggṛhītaṃ śailabhājane śailavan
                        mṛnmaye vā pātreṣv anuguptan nidadhyāt | tat sarvvakālam upayuñjīta |
                        tasyālābhe bhaumaṃ | tat punaḥ saptavidhaṃ | tad yathā kaupan nādeyaṃ
                        sārasan tāḍāga m prāsravaṇam audbhijaṃ cauṇṭyam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.45.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra varṣāvarṣāsvāntarikṣamaudbhijaṃ vā seveta mahāguṇatvā-t | śaradi
                        sarvvam prasannatvāt | hemante sārasan tāḍāgam vā | vasante kaupaṃ cauṇṭyaṃ
                        prāsrāvaṇam vā | grīṣme 'pyevaṃ | prāvṛṣyendram anabhivṛṣṭaṃ sarvvaṃ eva | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.45.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kīṭamūtrapurīṣāṇḍaśava-kothapradūṣitaṃ | tṛṇaparṇṇodakayutaṃ kaluṣam
                        viṣasaṃyutaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.10">

                        <caesura/>
                         yo 'vagāheta varṣāsu pibed vāpi navañ jalaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa bāhyābhyantarān rogān labhate kṣipram eva tu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.45.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra yat paṅkaśevālatṛṇahaṭhapadmaprabhṛtibhir avacchannaṃ
                        raviśaśikiraṇānilair vvātijuṣṭāṃ gandharasopasṛṣṭan tad vyāpannam iti vidyāt
                        | sparśarasarūpagandhavīryavipākāḥ | doṣāḥ ṣaṭ kharatā paicchilyam auṣṇyaṃ
                        dantagrāhitā ca sparśadoṣaḥ | paṅkasikatāśaivālavāhulyādvikṛtavarṇṇatā
                        rūpadoṣaḥ | vyaktarasatā rasadoṣaḥ | aniṣṭagandhatā gandhadoṣaḥ | yad
                        upayuktan tṛṣṇāgauravaśūlakaphaprasekān āpādayati sa vīryadoṣaḥ | yad
                        upayuktaṃ cirād vipacyate viṣṭambhayati sa vipākadoṣaḥ || ta ete āntarikṣe
                        doṣā na bhavanti | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.12">

                        <caesura/>

                        prasādhakam bhavati</l>

                        sādhāraṇatvāt | tatra sahyaprabhavāḥ kuṣṭhañ janayanti | vindhyaprabhavā
                        kuṣṭhaṃ hṛdrogañ ca | malayaprabhavāḥ krimīn | mahendraprabhavāḥ

                <div n="46" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 46, draft based on MS H]</head>




                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto 'nnapānavidhim vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dhanvantarim abhivādya suśruta uvāca ||
                        <caesura/>
                         bhagavan prāgabhihitam prāṇināṃ mūlam āhāro balavarṇṇaujasāñ ca saḥ ṣaṭsu
                        raseṣv āyatto rasāḥ punar dravyāśrayiṇaḥ | dravyarasavīryavipākanimitte ca
                        kṣayavṛddhī doṣāṇāṃ sātmyañ ca | brahmāder api ca lokasyāhāraḥ
                        sthityutpattihetur āhārādevābhivṛddhir balam ārogyavarṇendriyaprasādaś ca |
                        tathā hy āhāravaiṣampādasvāsthyan tasyāsitapītalīḍhakhāditasya
                        nānādravyātmakasyānekavidhavikalpaprabhāvasya pṛthak pṛthak
                        dravyarasavīryavipākakarmmecchāṃ jñātuṃ na hy anavabuddhadravyasvabhāvā
                        bhiṣajo roganigrahaṅ karttuṃ samarthā ity āhārāyattāś ca prāṇino yasmāt
                        tasmād annapānavidhim upadiśat tu me bhagavān ity uktaḥ provāca bhagavān
                        dhanvantariḥ
                        <caesura/>
                         || atha khalu vatsa suśruta || </l>



                    <!-- <lg type="varga"> -->

                    <p ana="subsubheading" style="bold">[<hi>Śālivarga</hi>]</p>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.4">

                        <caesura/>
                         tatra
                        lohitakaśālikalamakakarddamakapāṇḍukasugandhakasakunāhṛtakuṣmāṇḍakapuṇḍarīkamahāśāliśītabhīrukalodhraśūkadīrghaśūkakāñcanakahāyanakadūṣīmahākhyaprabhṛtayaḥ
                        śālayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         madhurā vīryataḥ śītā vipākā kaṭukāḥ smṛtāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittaghnālpānilakaphaḥ snigdhā vaddhālpavarccasaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.6">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmād alpāntaraguṇāḥ kramaśaḥ śālayo pare || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ṣaṣṭikakāṅgakamukundakapītakapramodakakālakāsanapuṣpakamahāsvetakamahāvrīhicūrṇṇakakuravakedāraprabhṛtayo
                        vrīhayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.9</label>
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         śālīnāṅguṇataś cāpi samānā vaddhavarccasaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ṣaṣṭikaḥ pravaras teṣāṅ kaṣāyānuraso laghuḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mṛduḥ snigdhas tridoṣaghnaḥ sthairyakṛdvalavarddhanaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rasato madhuragrāhī tulyo lohitaśālibhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śeṣās tv alpāntarās tv asmād vrīhayaḥ kramaśo guṇaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛṣṇavrīhiśālāmukhalāvākṣajātumukhanandīmukhatvaritakakurkkuṭāṇḍakapārāvatakapāṭalāprabhṛ<cb
                            n="2"/>tayo vrīhayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyamadhurāḥ pāke madhurā vīryato 'himāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         alpābhiṣyandinas tulyāḥ ṣaṣṭikair vvalavarddhanāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.14">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.15">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.34">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.34</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         māṣo gururbbhinnapurīṣamūtraḥ snigdho 'tha vṛṣyo madhuro 'nilaghnaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         santarppaṇaḥ stanyakaro viśeṣād valapradaḥ śukrakaphāvahaś ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.35">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         svādurvripāke madhuronasāndraḥ santarppaṇastanyarucipradaś ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.36">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.36</label>
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         āraṇyamāṣā guṇataḥ pradiṣṭā rūkṣāḥ kaṣāyā avidāhinaś ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.37">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.37</label>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.38">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         valāsa hantā nayanāmayaghno viśeṣato vanyakulattha uktaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.39">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.39</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         īṣatkaṣāyo madhuraḥ satiktaḥ sāṃgrāhikaḥ pittakarās tathoṣṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tilo vipake kaṭūko valiṣṭhaḥ snigdho vraṇo lepana pathyād uktaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.40">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.40</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dantyo 'gnimedhājanano 'lpamūtraḥ svaryo 'tha keśyo 'nilahā guruś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         tileṣu sarvvaṣ eva sitaḥ pradhāno madhyaḥ sito hīnatarās tathānye || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.41">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.41</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yavaxkaṣāyo madhuro himaś ca kaṭur vvipāke kaphapittahantā |
                        <caesura/>
                         vraṇeṣu pathyāstilavac ca nityaṃ pravṛddhamūtro bahuvātavarccāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.42">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.42</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sthairyāgnimedhāsvaravarṇṇakṛc ca sapicchilaḥ sthūlavilekhanaś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         medo 'nilastṛtṛraṇo 'tha rūkṣaḥ prasādanaḥ śoṇitapittayoś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.43">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.43</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ebhir gguṇair hīnataraiś ca kiñcid vidyād yavebhyo 'pi yavān aśeṣān |
                        <caesura/>
                         godhūma ukto madhuro guruś ca valyaḥ sthiraḥ śukravalapradaś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.44">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.44</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snigdho 'tha śīto 'nilapittahantā sandhānakṛc chleṣmakaraḥ saraś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         rūkṣaḥ kaṣāyo viṣaśokhaśukravalāsadṛṣṭikṣayakṛdvidāhī || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.45">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.45</label>
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         śitāśitā pītakinaḥ kuvarṇṇā bhavanti ye 'nyekisarāś ca simvāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.46">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.46</label>
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.47">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.47</label>
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.48">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.48</label>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.49">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.49</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         uṣṇātasī svādurasānilaghnī pittolvaṇā syāt kaṭukā vipāke |
                        <caesura/>
                         pāke rase cāpi kaṭupradiṣṭa ssiddhārthakaḥ śoṇitapittakopī || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.49ef">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.49ef</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snigdhoṣṇatiktaḥ kaphavātahantā tathā guṇaś cāśitasarṣapo pi || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.52">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.52</label>
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <!-- <lg type="varga"> -->

                    <p ana="subheading" style="bold">[<hi>Māṃsavarga</hi>]</p>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.53">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.53</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ata ūrddhvam māṃsavarggam upadekṣyāmaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra jaleśayā anūpā grāmyāḥ | kravyabhuja | ekasaphajāṅgalāś ceti |
                        ṣaṇmāṃsavarggā bhavanti | teṣām uttarottarāḥ pradhānatamās te punar dvividhā
                        ānūpajāṅgalāś ca | tatra jāṅgalavarggo 'ṣṭavidhaḥ | tatra jaṃghālā viṣkirāḥ
                        pranudā guheśayāḥ prasahāḥ parṇṇamṛgāḥ | vileśayā grāmyāś ceti || teṣañ
                        jaṅghālaviṣkirau pradhānatamau | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.54">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.54</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra jaṅghalā eṇahariṇarkuraṅga ṛṣya
                        rālakṛtamālaśalabhaśvadaṃṣṭrīcāruṣkavṛṣatemṛgamātṛkāprabhṛtayaḥ kaṣāya
                        madhurā laghavo vātapittaharās tīkṣṇā bastiviśodhanāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.55">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.46.55</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyamadhurā hṛdyaḥ pittāsṛkkapharogahā |
                        <caesura/>
                         sāṅgrāhī rocano valyas teṣām eṇo jvarāpahaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.56">

                         kecit piṣṭapayasy āhur anupānaṃ sukhodakaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.432">

                        <caesura/>
                         tatra pūrvvaśasya jā tānām vedarāmlaṃ | vaidalānān dhāmlaṃ | jāṅgalānān
                        mṛgānān dhanvajānām pakṣiṇāñ ca pippalyāsavaḥ | viṣkirāṇāṃ kolavadarāsavaḥ |
                        pratudānāṃ kṣīravṛksāsavaḥ | guhe śayānāṃ kharjjūranālikerāsavaḥ |
                        sāmudrāṇām mātuluṅgāsavaḥ | kus̤māṇḍānām amlānām sārdvīkāsavaḥ | amlā
                        amlānāṃ phalānāṃ padmotpalakandāsavaḥ | kaṣāyāṇāṃ dāḍimavetrāsavaḥ |
                        madhurāṇāṃ trikaṭukayuktaḥ khadirāsavaḥ | tālaphalādīnāṃ dhānyāmlaṃ |
                        kandānāṃ dūrvvānalavetrāsavaḥ | pippalyādīnāṃ svadaṃṣṭrāvasukāsavaḥ |
                        cuccūprabhṛtīnāṃ lodhrāsavaḥ | kusumbhaśākasya tad eva | maṇḍūkaparṇyādīnām
                        mahāpañcamūlyāsavaḥ | tālamastakādīnām amlaphalāsavaḥ | saindhavādīnāṃ
                        surāsavam āranālan toyam vā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.448">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.449">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.450">

                        <caesura/>
                         dravāṇi rasāś caiva rājateṣūpahārayet |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.451">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.452">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.453">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.454">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.455">

                         na caikarasasevāyāṃ prasajye ca kadācana ||
                        <caesura/>
                         śākāvarānnabhūyiṣṭhaṃ vyamlañ ca na samācaret | </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.491">

                        <caesura/>
                         ekaikaśaḥ samastām vā nāśnīyāc ca kadācana ||
                        <caesura/>
                         prāgbhukte 'py avivikte 'gnau dvirannan na samācaret | </l>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         annan na pākaṃ bhajate narasya || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.500"/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
